<tr class="thead">
<th aria-label="Rk" class="tooltip ranker sort_default_asc show_partial_when_sorting center" data-stat="ranker" data-tip="&lt;strong&gt;Rank&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;br&gt;This is a count of the rows from top to bottom.&lt;br&gt;It is recalculated following the sorting of a column.">Rk</th>

<tr class="thead">
<th aria-label="Rk" class="tooltip ranker sort_default_asc show_partial_when_sorting center" data-stat="ranker" data-tip="&lt;strong&gt;Rank&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;br&gt;This is a count of the rows from top to bottom.&lt;br&gt;It is recalculated following the sorting of a column.">Rk</th>

<th aria-label="Nation" class="sort_default_asc center" data-stat="nationality" data-tip="Nationality of the player.&lt;br&gt;First, we check our records in international play at senior level.&lt;br&gt;Then youth level.&lt;br&gt;Then citizenship presented on wikipedia.&lt;br&gt;Finally, we use their birthplace when available.">Nation</th>
